ARIE 1932-1933 [vol. 055]


A. List of copper-plates examined during the year 1932-33.


ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/1 (page 5)
Placement
The Collector of Tanjore
Dynasty
Vijayana-gara.
King
Śrīraṅgadēva-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1574 (expir-ed), Nandana, Tai 21, Monday, Uttiraṭṭādi, śu. pañchamī.
Language
Tamil
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
The plate belongs to the Trustee of the Kailāsanātha temple at Molaiyūr, Kumbakonam taluk. The characters are too modern for the date cited. Names of certain Vijayanagara kings are given without any order. Purports to register an agree-ment made among the resident-merchants of several villages of the Pandanallūr-śīrmai to pay imposts at certain rates per head-load on grains and other articles of merchandise, for providing for the daily offerings and worship in the temple of Kailāsanāthasvāmi and Saundariyammaṉ at Muḻaiyūr.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/2 (page 5)
Placement
The Zamindar of Punganur, through the Collector of Chittoor.
Dynasty
Suguṭūru
King
Immaḍi Chikkarāya Tam-maya-Gaunayya.
Date
Śaka 1648, Plava, Vaiśākha, śu. 5.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Records the agreement given to the chief by the Reḍḍis, Karṇams, Śeṭṭis and the 18 phaṇas of the several villages (in his estate), settling in cash the amount of annual rent to be paid by each village on its tobacco crops.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/3 (page 5)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Mummaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1725, Rudhi-rōdgāri, Śrāvaṇa, ba. 30, Wednes-day, solar eclipse.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the son of Immaḍi Chikkarāya and Dēvī-rammaṇṇi (the daughter of Vūlapāṭi Raṅgēgaunivāru) and the grandson of Mummaḍi Chikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra. Registers an endow-ment of lands made by the chief for the daily and special worships, offerings and lamps in the temple of Śiva built by him near Bhīmapuram attached to the Mōdugulapalle-sthala, and also the construction of a tank by him in the same place. Registers also the chief's renovation of the village-tank to the south of the temple, and his foundation of a garden near its bund. Records a supple-mentary gift of land made by the chief in Dhātu, on Āśvija, śu. 10, to the same temple.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/4 (page 6)
Placement
The Zamindar of Punganur, through the Collector of Chittoor.
Dynasty
Suguṭūru
King
Chikkarāya Tammaya-Gaunivāru.
Date
Śaka 1598, Naḷa, Śrāvaṇa, śu. 12.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
The letters are too modern for the date given in the record and are also indifferently engraved. Purports to register a cowl given by the chief to four persons granting as dasavandam half of the produce on the lands irrigated by a tank dug by them at Sōmulavirigi-pēṇṭa-sthala in Āvulapalle-sīma. The inscription bears at the end the signature ‘Chikarāyalu’.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/5 (page 6)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Immaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1675, Śrī-mukha, Māgha, śu, 10.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the grand-son of Suguṭūru Immaḍi Chikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra and the son of Mummaḍi Chikkarāya and his wife Mañjammaṇṇi, the daughter of Liṅgana-Gaunivāru of Baira-kūru. Registers the gift of lands made by the chief for the several services and festivals in the temple of Śiva (Mṛityuñ-jayēśvara) built by him at Chauḍēpalle.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/6 (page 6)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Mummaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1722, Raudri, Māgha, śu. 15, Thursday.
Language
Telugu
Origin
Returned to the Collector.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the grand-son of Suguṭūru Mummaḍi Chikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra and the son of Immaḍi Chikkarāya and his wife Dēvīrammaṇṇi who was the daughter of Vūlapāṭi Raṅgē-Gaunivāru. Registers the con-struction of a Śiva (Chandra-śēkharasvāmin) temple and a tank near Rāmasamudram by the chief and the endow-ment of lands made by him to the same temple.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/7 (page 6)
Placement
Mr. S.T.Srinivasagopala-chari, B.A., M.L., Advocate, Madras.
Dynasty
Eastern Chāḷukya.
King
Vishṇuvardhana-Mahārāja
Date
...... Uttarā-yaṇa.
Language
Sanskrit (in Chāḷukyan characters)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
This is an odd plate of a set the remaining plates of which are missing. Refers to the king's father Maṅgi-Yuvarāja by the title Abhilashitakārya-Vijaya-siddhi. Registers the tax-free grant of a land sowable with 12 khaṇḍikas of kōdrava seed made by the king to the scholar Vṛiddha-śarman well-versed in the three Vēdas, who was the son of Rēva-śarman and grand-son of Śaṅkara-śarman of the Hārīti-gōtra and Āpastamba-sūtra and was a resident of Vaṅgipaṟu.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/8 (page 7)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Achyutadēva-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1459, Hēma-lamba, Kārttika, śu. Utthāna-dvādaśī.
Language
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Registers the sarvamānya grant of the village Śeruvañjūru renamed Achyutēndramahā-rāyapuram situated in Nandi-vala-sīma in Kōnādi-nāḍu, a subdivision of Reṇḍāyiravēlip-paṟṟu in Śeṅgāṭṭu-kōṭṭam, a district in the Chandragiri-rājya of Jayaṅkoṇḍachōḷa-maṇḍalam, divided into shares among several learned Brāhmaṇas of various gōtras and sūtras. The grant is said to have been made by the king in the presence of God Viṭṭhalēśvara on the bank of the Tuṅga-bhadrā, at the request of Timmappa-Nāyaka.
ARIE/1932-1933/A/1932-33/9 (page 7)
Placement
Mr. T. Krishna Aiyangar, Village Munsiff, Kollan-kondan, Srivillipputtur taluk, Ramnad district.
Dynasty
Later Pāṇḍya.
King
Jaṭilavarman alias Tribhu-vanachakravartin Kōnē-[ri]ṉmaikoṇḍāṉ Abhirāma Ativīrarāma Śrīvallabha.
Date
19th year, Śaka 1503, Vṛisha, Uttarāyaṇa, Grī-shma-ṛitu, Mithuna 24, ba. 5, Wednesday, Śatabhishaj, Saubhāgya-yōga, Taitila-karaṇa.
Language
Sanskrit in Grantha
Origin
Returned to the owner.
Edition
South Indian Inscriptions.
Remarks
Registers the grant made by Abhirāma-Sundarēśa Vara-tuṅgarāma, who was the son of Kulaśēkharadēva Parākrama-Pāṇḍyadēva of the Ātrēya-gōtra and was born in the Pushya-nakshatra, of the village Śōlaiśēri alias Nayinā-ragaram in Āṇmaṟai-nāḍu, as an agrahāra to Brāhmaṇas of various gōtras and sūtras, under the new name Śivakāma-sundari-chaturvēdimaṅgalam given to it in honour of his queen. Refers to the donor's elder brother Guṇarāma.

Dynasty
Pāṇḍya
King

Date
12th year, Mārgaḻi
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers gift of cows and calves for a twilight lamp in the temple of Tirumallīśvramuḍaiya-Nāyaṉār at Āṟṟūr alias Rājarājanallūr in Āṟṟūr-nāḍu, a subdivision of Ūṟṟukkāṭṭu-kōṭṭam, by a resident of the village.
ARIE/1932-1933/B/1932-33/3 (page 8)
Placement
On one of the steps leading to the moat, near the Āñjanēya temple.
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Śrīraṅgarāyadēva-Mahārāya ‘ruling from Vidyānagara’.
Date
Śaka 15[02], Vikrama, Kārtika, śu. 12.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the gift of the village Meyyūr in Cheṅgalpaṭṭu-sīma situated in the amaram of Maṇḍalēśvara Rāmarāja Veṅkaṭapatirājayyadēva-Mahārāja as sarvamānya for the daily, monthly and car festivals of god Raghu-nāyaka at Cheṅgalipaṭṭupāḷem during the administra-tion of the division by Viśvanāthayyavāru under Daḷavāyi Tirumala-Nāyanivāru.

ARIE/1932-1933/B/1932-33/13 (page 9)
Placement
On two stones lying near the same temple.
Dynasty
Do.
King
[Lost]
Date
[Lost]
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Fragmentary. Commences with the introduction ‘Tirumagaḷpōla’, etc., of Rājarāja I. Mentions an ugachchaṉ of Tirumukkūḍal, the northern hamlet of Madhurāntaka-chaturvēdimaṅgalam, and records a grant of money made to the temple. Near these stones is another inscription in modern characters dated in [Kali] 4375 (wrong), which states that this temple was renovated by Subbarāya-Mudali of Tiruvēṟkāḍu, son of Rāmaliṅga-Mudali of the Killiyādri-Mahārishi-gōtra, who claims to be a descendant of [Śīraga-Nāyaṉār ?] one of the 63 saints celebrated in the Periyapurāṇam.
ARIE/1932-1933/B/1932-33/14 (page 9)
Placement
Nemmali.--On the north and west walls of the Muktīśvara temple.

Pāṇḍya
King

Date
8th year, Kumbha, śu. 1, Monday, Śadaiyam.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers a grant of tax-free land by the (community of) Tamiḻadaraiyar of Kaḷattūr in Kaḷattūr-kōṭṭam, a district of Jayaṅkoṇḍaśōḻa-maṇḍalam to the temple of Avimuktīśvaram-uḍaiya-Nāyaṉār in their kāṇi village Neṉmali alias Puṇḍarīkanallūr situated in Valla-nāḍu in the same kōṭṭam for offerings, etc., to the image of Puṇḍarīka-Nāyaka set up in the temple by a Śivabrāhmaṇa.

38th year (in figures and in words).
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Commences with the introduction Pugaḻmāduviḷaṅga, etc., after a few words beginning with ‘Vīramē-tuṇaiyā-gavum’. Registers the gift of oil made by the Nagarattār of Rājēndraśōḻapuram in Maiyyūr-nāḍu, a subdivision of Kaḷattūr-kōṭṭam for a perpetual lamp in the temple of Tiruppataṅgāḍuḍaiya-Mahā-dēva at Rājēndraśōḻanallūr in Pālaiyūr-nāḍu.

Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers the royal order, issued at the instance of Nandiyarāyar, remitting certain taxes in kind and coin due on some dēvadāna lands belonging to the temple of Tiruppataṅgāḍ-Uḍaiyār for worship and repairs therein. The document is signed by nine officers including the Royal Secretary.

Kali 4540, Siddhār-thi, Mīna, śu. 14, Thursday, Hasta.
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Registers a tax-free grant of land at Villiyaṉpākkam as dēvadāna for offerings, etc., in the temple of Tiruttokkī-śuram-Uḍaiyār of the village, by Tipparāja of Āṟṟūr-pāḷaiyam, the son of Koṇḍaikavundirāja of the lunar race, and Sēnāpatippiḷḷai, the agent of Hanumanta-rāja of Tenkaḻaṉippaṭṭupāḷaiyam (in Pulippākkam), who was the son of Sāḷuva Hanumanta-Rāmarāja of the same race.

ARIE/1932-1933/B/1932-33/76 (page 15)
Placement
On stones built into the north and west walls of the same temple.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Rājarājakēsarivarman, ‘who destroyed the ships at Śālai.’
Date
14th year, 32nd day (in words).
Language
Tamil
Remarks
Portions lost. Registers a gift of land by the Mahā-sabhā of Āṉiyūr in Kaḷattūr-kōṭ am as bhaṭta-vṟitti to a brahman (name lost) of the village, well-versed in one Vēda besides the Sāma-Vēda, in the Pāṇini grammar, in the Mīmāṁsā, etc., without detriment to the money-income due therefrom to the Subrahmaṇya temple at Tiruttaṇi, to which this land had originally been assign-ed. The donee was to teach these subjects to four pupils and feed them daily. There are three more frag-ments, one of which seems to record provision made for playing musical instruments during the several services in the temple; another is a part of a record of Pārthivēndrava[rman] and the third, of Rājarāja I.

Remarks
Refers to Origāṇḍi Rēmana of the Śrīvatsa-gōtra who was the minister of king Rājēndra-Chōḍa and was appointed by him the governor of Kamma-dēśa. His son was Drōṇa, whose son by his wife Prōlāmbikā was Kumāra (called also Komma) who was the minister of Goṅka, the son of Chōḍa (i.e. Rājēndra-Chōḍa). Komma is stated to have built the temple of Kumārēśvara and constructed the tank called Drōṇasamudra at Nārāyaṇapāḍu. Registers the grant of lands made for the offerings of the god and to Brahmans, and the gift of 55 sheep for a perpetual lamp to the god Sōmēśvaradēva of the village, by the same minister who is called also Mandadi Kommanā-mātya who is styled the ‘lord of the town of Origāṇḍi.’

Registers a gift of land made by the king to his guru Kalyāṇaśakti of the Kāḷāmukha sect for the worship, offerings, etc., of the god Guruliṅgadēva installed by the latter in the temple of Padmēśvara, constructed by the king in memory of his mother Padmaladēvī. Mentions Mahāpradhāna Dāsirāja, an officer of the king.
ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/54 (page 97)
Placement
Haraḷahaḷḷi--Slab set up against the front wall of the house of Honnappa Byāḍagi.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Do. ‘ruling Banavāse-nāḍu from his capital at Guttavoḷal’.
Date
Śaka 1110, Plavaṅga, Phālguṇa, śu. 13, Thursday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
States that Mahāpradhāna Daṇḍanāyaka Dāsirāja constructed the temple of Dāsēśvara at Sōmeśvara-pura and on lowed it with land, after purchasing it from the king. Records a gift of the village Kodaḷiya Hosivūru in Perbbāḷa-Seventy, made by the Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Mācharasa to Rājaguru Kalyāṇa-śaktidēva. Also registers a grant of the village Koṇṇaji in Noḷambavāḍi, made to the same temple by Jagadēva-Pāṇḍya, after its purchase from Dāsirāja, on the occasion of his coronation and the gift of the village (name lost) made by Sōmaladēvī, Dēvarasa, etc., on the occasion of the coronation of Vijaya-Pāṇḍyadēva, son of Oḍeyarasadēva. The recipient of the gifts was Kalyāṇaśaktidēva.

Records the gift of money made by Vishṇuvardhana Bīchi-Śeṭṭi, for the worship of the god Yamēśvara-dēva.

ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/184 (page 109)

Rāshṭr-kūṭa.
King
Nitya[varsha] Niru[pama]-Vallaha.

Śaka 840 (in words), [Bahu]dhānya, Śrāvaṇa, śu. sap-tamī, Sunday.

Kannaḍa
Remarks
Badly damaged. Seems to register a settlement made regarding the revenue of Baṭṭakeṟe, between Mahasrī-manta, the governor of Beḷvala Three Hundred, etc., and the Mahājanas of the place.
ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/185 (page 109)
Placement
Slab lying near the same prākāra (outside).
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikrama year 41, Dur-mukhi, Pushya, ba. 3, Sunday, Uttarāyaṇa-saṅ-kramaṇa, Vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers a gift of land made by Maṇiyara Mahādēvayya-Nāyaka after purchase from the Two Hundred Mahā-janas of Baṭṭakeṟe for the benefit of a satra and of the temple of Maṇiyara Mallikārjunadēva.
ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/186 (page 109)
Placement
Stone built into the same praka-ra (outside).
Dynasty
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Kṛishṇarāya-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1442, Pramā-din, Jyēshṭha, śu. 15, lunar eclipse.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
States that Nayanappa-Nāyaka, son of Bāgila Nāgi-Nāyaka granted land at Baṭṭarkeṟe in Gadugina-sīme, which was granted to the donor as umbaḷi by Tim-mappa-Nāyaka-Ayyanavaru, for the benefit of two water-sheds (aravaṭige). The grant was made in the presence of god Virūpāksha on the bank of the Tuṅgabhadrā.
ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/187 (page 109)
Placement
Another slab built into the same prākāra.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Bhūlōkamalladēva
Date
11th year, Naḷa, [Jyēshṭa], śu. 2, Monday, Saṅkrān-ti, Vyatīpāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Worn out. Registers a gift of land and money made by the Brahman Chauḍeyadēva, for worship and offerings to the god Hṛishīkēśadēva of Kāḷimayyagēri, when the One Thousand Mahājanas of the Mahāgrahāra Lokkiguṇḍi, headed by the Ūroḍeya, were administer-ing the dharma. Also records minor gifts made to the god Kēśavadēva of Kāḷimayyagēri.

DHARWAR DISTRICT


ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/188 (page 110)
Placement
A third slab built into the same prākāra.
Dynasty
Western Chāḷukya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikrama year 25, Vikrama, Māgha, śu. 5, Sunday, Uttarāya-ṇa-saṅkramaṇa, Vyatīpāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Badly damaged. Records the construction of the temple of Śaṅkara-Nārāyaṇadēva, of a tank and a satra by Maddimayya-Nāyaka, and registers gifts of land and money made by him for worship, etc., to the god and the upkeep of the tank and the satra. Also records a gift made by the One Thousand Mahājanas of Lokki-guṇḍi.
ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/189 (page 110)
Placement
Slab built into a drain behind a Brahmin's house near the same temple.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Traiḷōkyamalladēva
Date
Śaka 986, Krōdhi, ...., lunar eclipse.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged and mutilated. In later characters. Pro-bably a copy. Seems to register a gift of land made by Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Chōḷaṅgoh2ḍa Mārarasa, while governing Beḷvoḷa Three Hundred, etc., to Tatpurasha-Jīya for the benefit of a temple (name lost), a maṭha, the ascetics, etc.

ARIE/1932-1933/D/1932-33/192 (page 110)

King
Bhūlōkamalladēva
Date
…
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Fragment. Mentions Ummachige as an agrahara in Nareyaṅgal [Twelve] included in Beḷvala, and refers to the Brahman Māhaṇāryya, the brother of Padmaṇa and son of Jēmaṇa born in the Chānura-vaṁśa.
